  <div class="markdown-body f5 mb-2">
    <p>The Jupyter Notebook is a language-agnostic HTML notebook application for Project Jupyter. Jupyter notebooks are documents that allow for creating and sharing live code, equations, visualizations, and narrative text together. People use them for data cleaning and transformation, numerical simulation, statistical modeling, data visualization, machine learning, and much more.</p>

                  <p>In the <a href="https://github.com/jakevdp/PythonDataScienceHandbook/blob/master/notebooks/05.09-Principal-Component-Analysis.ipynb">PCA section</a> there is the following quote:</p>
<blockquote>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/47821203/53817403-442fc300-3f5d-11e9-9478-059f7b9afc53.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/47821203/53817403-442fc300-3f5d-11e9-9478-059f7b9afc53.png" alt="image" style="max-width:100%;"></a><br>
We see that these 150 components account for just over 90% of the variance.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>While not inaccurate (150 componen</p>

              <a class="text-gray-dark" href="https://github.com/CamDavidsonPilon/Probabilistic-Programming-and-Bayesian-Methods-for-Hackers/issues/493" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;explore.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;click_context&quot;:&quot;REPOSITORY_CARD&quot;,&quot;click_target&quot;:&quot;ISSUE&quot;,&quot;click_visual_representation&quot;:&quot;BIG_GOOD_FIRST_ISSUE&quot;,&quot;actor_id&quot;:60628828,&quot;record_id&quot;:593987514,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/topics/jupyter-notebook&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:60628828}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="feebef48a7f34dbe31723a4e4eceee5e2e211bc284404c219eb32e0673844771" data-ga-click="Explore, go to issue, location:good first issues;size:large;">
                normed option in plt.hist is deprecated
</a>

            </h1>

          <div class="mr-3">
            <img
              class="avatar avatar-user avatar-small"

            <div class="Box Box--condensed position-relative timeline-comment--caret">
              <div class="Box-header f6 text-gray">
                <strong class="text-gray-dark text-bold">
                  ecotner
                </strong>

                  commented

                <relative-time datetime="2020-04-04T18:27:03Z" class="no-wrap">Apr 4, 2020</relative-time>
              </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>I just started going through the jupyter notebooks (great stuff, by the way), and when running the cells the first time I would always get some error like <code>Polygon has no attribute normed</code>. It turns out that the <code>normed</code> option in <code>plt.hist</code> has been deprecated (in <code>matplotlib</code> version 3.1.1 and later as far as I can tell), and should instead be replaced with <code>density</code> (they appear to operate simi</p>

                    class="position-absolute right-0 left-0 bottom-0 text-center"
                    style="background: linear-gradient(to top, rgba(255,255,255,1), rgba(255,255,255,0));"

                      Read more
</a>                  </div>

            <div class="Box Box--condensed position-relative timeline-comment--caret">
              <div class="Box-header f6 text-gray">
                <strong class="text-gray-dark text-bold">
                  alqbib
                </strong>

                  commented

                <relative-time datetime="2019-03-31T09:31:13Z" class="no-wrap">Mar 31, 2019</relative-time>
              </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <h1>Vectorized version of gradient descent.</h1>
<p>theta = theta * reg_param - alpha * (1 / num_examples) * (delta.T @ self.data).T</p>
<h1>We should NOT regularize the parameter theta_zero.</h1>
<p>theta[0] = theta[0] - alpha * (1 / num_examples) * (self.data[:, 0].T @ delta).T</p>
<p>the first code line ,theta include theta[0].<br>
so I think can write like this:<br>
theta[0] -= alpha * (1 / num_examples) * (self.data[:, 0].</p>

                  <div
                    class="position-absolute right-0 left-0 bottom-0 text-center"
                    style="background: linear-gradient(to top, rgba(255,255,255,1), rgba(255,255,255,0));"

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <h3>Description</h3>
<p>Add Azure notebook to our SETUP doc.<br>
I tested google colab and Azure notebook to run reco-repo without requiring creating any DSVM or compute by myself, and it works really well with simple tweaks to the notebooks (e.g. for some libs, should install manually).</p>
<p>I think it would be good to add at least Azure notebook to our SETUP doc, where users can easily test out our repo w/o</p>

            <h1 class="d-inline flex-auto f3 text-normal lh-condensed">
              <a class="text-gray-dark" href="https://github.com/dunovank/jupyter-themes/issues/381" data-hydro-click="{&quot;event_type&quot;:&quot;explore.click&quot;,&quot;payload&quot;:{&quot;click_context&quot;:&quot;REPOSITORY_CARD&quot;,&quot;click_target&quot;:&quot;ISSUE&quot;,&quot;click_visual_representation&quot;:&quot;BIG_GOOD_FIRST_ISSUE&quot;,&quot;actor_id&quot;:60628828,&quot;record_id&quot;:584306206,&quot;originating_url&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/topics/jupyter-notebook&quot;,&quot;user_id&quot;:60628828}}" data-hydro-click-hmac="23c4d8289633405eb55a208a7ca97f426f5154a05fb9ded937b077c5da858af9" data-ga-click="Explore, go to issue, location:good first issues;size:large;">
                In README.md replace reference to &quot;stylish&quot; brower extension with &quot;stylus&quot; because of malware issues
</a>

            </h1>
          </div>

        </div>

        <div class="d-flex">
          <div class="mr-3">
            <img
              class="avatar avatar-user avatar-small"
              alt="jeanmonet"
              src="https://avatars1.githubusercontent.com/u/15112920?v=4"
              width="32"
              height="32"
            >
          </div>
          <div class="flex-auto" style="width: 80%;">
            <div class="Box Box--condensed position-relative timeline-comment--caret">
              <div class="Box-header f6 text-gray">
                <strong class="text-gray-dark text-bold">
                  jeanmonet
                </strong>

                  commented

                <relative-time datetime="2020-03-19T10:21:40Z" class="no-wrap">Mar 19, 2020</relative-time>
              </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>It appears that the "stylish" browser extension is now considered to be spyware. See:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://meta.stackoverflow.com/a/294045/11750716" rel="nofollow">https://meta.stackoverflow.com/a/294045/11750716</a> (end of post)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/openstyles/stylus/wiki/FAQ#what-are-the-main-differences-and-improvements-over-the-original-stylish-add-on">https://github.com/openstyles/stylus/wiki/FAQ#what-are-the-main-differences-and-improvements-over-the-original-stylish-add-on</a></li>
</ul>
<p>Please replace with a reference to "stylus" browser extension.</p>

                  <div
                    class="position-absolute right-0 left-0 bottom-0 text-center"

                  <p>fig.append_trace() raises ValueError if the row arg is not type int, even if arg is int-like:<br>
DEBUG row:1, type(row):&lt;class 'numpy.int64'&gt;</p>

1535</p>

              <div class="Box-header f6 text-gray">
                <strong class="text-gray-dark text-bold">
                  holgersson32644
                </strong>

                  commented

                <relative-time datetime="2020-05-02T17:09:17Z" class="no-wrap">May 2, 2020</relative-time>
              </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>Hi, I stumbled over a bug resp. mistake in your documentation.</p>
<h3>Bug description</h3>
<p>Your setup documentation contains call of</p>
<p><code>sudo echo something &gt; file</code></p>
<p>which is ..well..entirely wrong. sudo echo will write to stdout, then the redirection with "&gt;" will write it with user rights and this will fail as this example wants to add a debian repo to a location where only root can write.</p>

                  <div
                    class="position-absolute right-0 left-0 bottom-0 text-center"
                    style="background: linear-gradient(to top, rgba(255,255,255,1), rgba(255,255,255,0));"
                  >

                      Read more
</a>                  </div>
                </div>
            </div>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p><em>inspired by #101</em></p>
<p>Once we merge in new robustness transforms, <code>crop_to_size</code> should probably be in the default transforms. We still want to allow not passing it, but should probably warn in that case.</p>

                <relative-time datetime="2019-06-03T17:11:20Z" class="no-wrap">Jun 3, 2019</relative-time>

                <div class="Box-body comment-body markdown-body position-relative overflow-hidden pt-3" style="max-height:200px">
                  <p>Coming from a Python-in-Jupyter background, I notice that <code>Tab</code> works as you would expect (reveals all available methods/attributes), but <code>Shift+Tab</code> (signature hinting) does not. I could not find documentation on this. Is <code>Shift+Tab</code> not supported, or is my setup is incorrect?</p>
<p>Example:</p>
<pre><code>type Foo struct {
    name string
    description string
}
func (f Foo) Qux(s string) string {
   
</code></pre>

                    class="position-absolute right-0 left-0 bottom-0 text-center"
